If c1=0: T*c0/c2 + T*c3*log/c2 + c5*epsilon/c2 + c6*log/c2 + c7*epsilon/c2 + c8/c2

Basis: {T, T*log(c4*epsilon+1), epsilon, log(c4*epsilon+1), 1}

Missing: T*epsilon term! 

Candidate 43 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 46:
```
T²*c0*log/(T*c2+c3) + T*c4*log/(T*c2+c3) + T*c5*epsilon/(T*c2+c3) + c6*epsilon/(T*c2+c3) + c7*log/(T*c2+c3) + c8*epsilon/(T*c2+c3) + c9/(T*c2+c3)
```

If c2=0: T²*c0*log/c3 + T*c4*log/c3 + T*c5*epsilon/c3 + ... This has T²*log which GT doesn't have. Setting c0=0 removes it.

With c2=0, c0=0: T*c4*log/c3 + T*c5*epsilon/c3 + (c6+c8)*epsilon/c3 + c7*log/c3 + c9/c3

Basis: {T*log, T*epsilon, epsilon, log, 1} - missing standalone T.

Candidate 46 verdict: [NO MATCH]
